 ardhaya          
  
   āsāro dhārāsamapāto yata täna ṭīkāvehi asāraya dhārāya sampāta yayi padatrayak koṭa dakvatisannayehi hā amarakoṣādiyehi da asāraya dhārā sampātayayi padadvayak kereti  
  
   mē aḍḍha addha upaḍḍha yana śabdatraya asamabhāgayehi väṭenakalhi pulliṅguya  samabhāgayehi väṭenakalhi napuṃsakaliṅgu ättāhuyi  ema kīha ṭīkāvehi eteca aḍḍhādayo tayo asamabhāge pume same tu napuṃsake  
  
     the three words  aḍḍha  addha   and  upaḍḍha   when applied to uneual parts  are masculine  but when they denote eual parts  they are neuter and assume another form  as  aḍḍhaṃ  addhaṃ  upaḍḍhaṃ
